        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          margin: auto;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

        }

          flex-grow: 0;

        }

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Author: Andreas Haas <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Andreas Haas &lt;<!----></span>





ahaas@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/ahaas@chromium.org"><!---->ahaas@chromium.org<!----></a>

Date:   Wed Nov 30 17:21:04 2022 +0100



<span class="line"><!---->Date:   Wed Nov 30 17:21:04 2022 +0100<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    [d8] Make CPU profiling more thread-safe



<span class="line"><!---->    [d8] Make CPU profiling more thread-safe<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    The fuzzer had some issues with the initial CPU profiling code:



<span class="line"><!---->    The fuzzer had some issues with the initial CPU profiling code:<!----></span>



<br>





    * The CpuProfiler may get accessed from multiple workers/isolate/threads,



<span class="line"><!---->    * The CpuProfiler may get accessed from multiple workers/isolate/threads,<!----></span>



<br>





      which caused a use-after-free if the CpuProfiler gets disposed while



<span class="line"><!---->      which caused a use-after-free if the CpuProfiler gets disposed while<!----></span>



<br>





      some thread is still accessing it.



<span class="line"><!---->      some thread is still accessing it.<!----></span>



<br>





    * and profiling may not have been stopped before disposing the profiler,



<span class="line"><!---->    * and profiling may not have been stopped before disposing the profiler,<!----></span>



<br>





      which caused a use-after-free by the profiling thread which did not get



<span class="line"><!---->      which caused a use-after-free by the profiling thread which did not get<!----></span>



<br>





      stopped.



<span class="line"><!---->      stopped.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    The first issue was caused by storing a global `CpuProfiler*` in d8,



<span class="line"><!---->    The first issue was caused by storing a global `CpuProfiler*` in d8,<!----></span>



<br>





    which was shared among all threads. This pointer was needed to call



<span class="line"><!---->    which was shared among all threads. This pointer was needed to call<!----></span>



<br>





    `CollectSample`. The solution was to load the D8Console from the isolate,



<span class="line"><!---->    `CollectSample`. The solution was to load the D8Console from the isolate,<!----></span>



<br>





    and then load the `CpuProfiler*` from the D8Console. Thereby a thread



<span class="line"><!---->    and then load the `CpuProfiler*` from the D8Console. Thereby a thread<!----></span>



<br>





    always loads a thread-local `CpuProfiler*`, which is then guaranteed to



<span class="line"><!---->    always loads a thread-local `CpuProfiler*`, which is then guaranteed to<!----></span>



<br>





    exist.



<span class="line"><!---->    exist.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    The second issue was solved by calling `StopProfiler` before `Dispose`



<span class="line"><!---->    The second issue was solved by calling `StopProfiler` before `Dispose`<!----></span>



<br>





    if profiling was still ongoing.



<span class="line"><!---->    if profiling was still ongoing.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





    R=



<span class="line"><!---->    R=<!----></span>





clemensb@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/clemensb@chromium.org"><!---->clemensb@chromium.org<!----></a>
